2025-04-15T08:35:01.8988529Z  --- Check KSM (kernel memory deduper) --- 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025323Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025514Z Memory de-duplication instructions
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025781Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025996Z You have kernel memory de-duper (called Kernel Same-page Merging,
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026409Z or KSM) available, but it is not currently enabled.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026641Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026776Z To enable it run:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026975Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027145Z     echo 1 >/sys/kernel/mm/ksm/run
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027603Z     echo 1000 >/sys/kernel/mm/ksm/sleep_millisecs
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027943Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028164Z If you enable it, you will save 40-60% of netdata memory.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028544Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028709Z  --- Check apps.plugin --- 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066470Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066635Z apps.plugin needs privileges
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066912Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9067191Z Since you have installed netdata as a normal user, to have apps.plugin collect
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9067857Z all the needed data, you have to give it the access rights it needs, by running
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9068621Z either of the following sets of commands:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9068982Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9069202Z To run apps.plugin with escalated capabilities:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9069811Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9070161Z     sudo chown root:docker "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9070866Z     sudo chmod 0750 "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9071750Z     sudo setcap cap_dac_read_search,cap_sys_ptrace+ep "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072304Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072421Z or, to run apps.plugin as root:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072626Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072940Z     sudo chown root:docker "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9073625Z     sudo chmod 4750 "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074023Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074272Z apps.plugin is performing a hard-coded function of data collection for all
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074894Z running processes. It cannot be instructed from the netdata daemon to perform
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9075383Z any task, so it is pretty safe to do this.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9075607Z
